Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971

	THIS AGC PROGRAM SHALL ALSO BE REFERRED TO AS
				COLOSSUS 3
	THIS PROGRAM IS INTENDED FOR USE IN THE CM AS SPECIFIED
	IN REPORT R-577.  THIS PROGRAM WAS PREPARED UNDER OSR
	PROJECT 55-23890, SPONSORED BY THE MANNED SPACECRAFT
	CENTER OF THE NATIONAL AERONAUTICS AND SPACE
	ADMINISTRATION THROUGH CONTRACT NAS 9-4065 WITH THE
	CHARLES STARK DRAPER LABORATORY, MASSACHUSETTS INSTITUTE OF
	TECHNOLOGY, CAMBRIDGE, MASS.


000002,000002:                                                                                                 #  Copyright:     Public domain.
000003,000003:                                                                                                 #  Filename:      MAIN.agc
000004,000004:                                                                                                 #  Purpose:       Part of the source code for Artemis (i.e., Colossus 3),
000005,000005:                                                                                                 #                 build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM) 
000006,000006:                                                                                                 #                 Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), we believe for 
000007,000007:                                                                                                 #                 Apollo 15-17.
000008,000008:                                                                                                 #  Assembler:     yaYUL
000009,000009:                                                                                                 #  Contact:       Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
000010,000010:                                                                                                 #  Website:       www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
000011,000011:                                                                                                 #  Page scans:    www.ibiblio.org/apollo/ScansForConversion/Artemis072/
000012,000012:                                                                                                 #  Mod history:   2004-12-21 RSB  Created.
000013,000013:                                                                                                 #                 2005-05-14 RSB  Corrects website reference above.
000014,000014:                                                                                                 #                 2009-07-25 RSB  Fixups for this header so that it can
000015,000015:                                                                                                 #                                 be used for code conversions.
000016,000016:                                                                                                 #                 2009-08-12 JL   Fix typo.
000017,000017:                                                                                                 #                 2009-08-18 JL   Change some filenames to match log section names.
000018,000018:                                                                                                 #                 2009-09-03 JL   Comment out some modules that are not available yet, 
000019,000019:                                                                                                 #                                 to start checking build.
000020,000020:                                                                                                 #                 2009-09-04 JL   Uncomment modules that are now available.
000021,000021:                                                                                                 #                 2010-02-20 RSB  The effects of most of the ## in this header were
000022,000022:                                                                                                 #                                 horrible, so I removed them ... and in all of the
000023,000023:                                                                                                 #                                 other included source files as well.
000024,000024:                                                                                                 #                 
000025,000025:                                                                                                 #  MAIN.agc is a little different from the other Artemis072 files  
000026,000026:                                                                                                 #  provided, in that it doesn't represent anything that appears 
000027,000027:                                                                                                 #  directly in the original source.  What I (RSB) have done for 
000028,000028:                                                                                                 #  organizational purposes is to split the huge monolithic source 
000029,000029:                                                                                                 #  code into smaller, more manageable chunks--i.e., into individual
000030,000030:                                                                                                 #  source files.  Those files are rejoined within this file as 
000031,000031:                                                                                                 #  "includes".  It just makes it a little easier to work with.  The
000032,000032:                                                                                                 #  code chunks correspond to natural divisions into sub-programs.  
000033,000033:                                                                                                 #  The divisions are by the assembly listing itself.
